< review>
The owners and staff here are truly wonderful, and the wine very good. It's a small winery who truly cares about their products, which is refreshing since so many wineries in Temecula are so corporate. It's a very nice change from dealing with employees who would much prefer to be somewhere else, and not having to fight your way to the tasting bar (if you visit on a weekend). Also, they welcome dogs like most wineries should, but don't anymore if they're too corporate.<//review>

<date>1502922464715</date><rating>2</rating>< text>
This place is not what it use to be. I've been a member of their club for over 4 years now and haven't been into the tasting room for 2 years. Always loved the wine and we order cases of it throughout the year. This past weekend I went into the tasting room with my parents and husband only for them to tell me that they could only comp 2 tastings. What type of wine club is this if the one time you make a special trip to go into the tasting room after spending thousands on their wine and they can't even comp a tasting. After arguing with the manager she finally agreed to it, after all when I signed the membership agreement it included 4 tastings. Super disappointed in what this winery has become.</text>

< Review>
This is the only place I've ever taken my car for my biennial smog check. As the name implies, it is a Star certified check station. They only do smog checks and not repairs. Gary is very knowledgeable and runs a tight shop. Even without an appointment I was in and out within twenty minutes. The technician, Kevin, was respectful, wore a mask, answered some of my questions regarding OBD2 monitors readiness. The shop offers a free retest within 14 days, or a 50% discount on your smog check after that time period. I'm always a little anxious and stressed out before getting my check, but it is a good feeling of relief to leave with that certificate that says "Passed". I would whole-heartedly recommend these guys!<//Review>

<userid>116612667142634595412<//userid><name>Rithwik Hari< /name><date>1572386530866< /date><Rate>5</Rate>< text>
This is one of my favorite spots in SF.

The pizza is fantastic (admittedly the only thing I've ordered aside from cheesecake which was also great). Thin crust, fantastic toppings like house made sausage, wild mushrooms, and Humboldt Fog goat cheese.

The owner used to be in the beer/wine business and always has a fantastic rotating selection of draft beers.

But on top of the actual food and drink, the environment at Kezar is incredible. I used to live in the neighborhood and would be there multiple times a week; nowadays, I try make the trek to Cole Valley every week to catch up with all the other regulars who I have gotten to know (including the owner Basim, who is a wonderful guy). There are TVs to watch the game, and there's usually great conversation to be had there if you're looking for it too. I can't count the number of times I've wandered into Kezar alone and left beaming after an unexpectedly great chat.

They have a large space in the back for big groups! Sometimes this place gets randomly swamped with a party of like 20 in the back which can hold up service, but otherwise service is prompt and friendly; the staff are all really kind.

If I ever leave the city, this is a place that I will always associate with SF. It is a special place; it feels like there aren't many establishments like this in SF nowadays. Definitely worth a visit, maybe I'll see you there sometime!</text>

< review>
I love this place SO MUCH. The first time I came here, I actually thought it was a bar from the outside. When I walked in I realized my mistake, but opted to stay anyway because it looked like they had some beer on tap. I'm so glad I did. They not only have incredible craft beers on tap (especially some heavy and delicious stouts/porters for those dark beer fans), they have a HUMBOLDT FOG PIZZA. If that doesn't sell you on this place I don't know what will.
The ambience is sort of strange here, but in the most charming way. There's a massive aquarium in the middle of the room that divides the place in half, a great but small bar that serves wine and some of the best tasting beer I've had in the bay, there's almost always a gaggle of circus performers from the circus school next door hanging out in the back unwinding after their classes, and the bar plays the strangest selection of music‚Äîsometimes it's EDM, sometimes 90's garage rock, you just never know. Oh, and the best damn pizza on earth, that mean Humboldt Fog Pizza. Definitely check it out, it's such a great little undiscovered gem of the inner sunset/ashbury/cole valley area.</review>

Third time here and just have to get a quick rating up here as it's quickly becoming one of my favourite spots. The quality of food and ingredients is so high for what otherwise appears to be a quintessentially perfect neighborhood bar. There used to be more places like this in San Francisco that were comfortable, welcoming, unpretentious, somewhat quirky (e.g. fish tank), and second to none in quality.

I have a birthday coming up and can't think of any place I'd rather invite 20 friends meet at to eat, drink and laugh. There's a loungey area in the back that seems perfect for such a meet up...

Anyways, go there and help keep places like this open in SF.< /review>

<Rate>4<//Rate><gmap_id>0x80dc79f4c7f4a999:0x6b7146212f532f67</gmap_id>< Time>
1535254878478</Time>
<Review>An Oceanside secret to share. I sometimes forget how many hidden gems Oceanside has to offer and this is one of them. You can get your wine tasting fix without having to go very far if you already live in North County. This location grows their own grapes and has a pretty wide selection of varietals to taste, some of which I believe were sourced elsewhere. Don't quote me on that.

The atmosphere is chill and the traffic is steady but not stuffy. Depending on how busy the owners are, you can get some quality time with them and learn about how their winery came to fruition. It's a nice story. The deck is open and has views of the land. I tried looking for Jason Mraz's house but couldn't quite see it. Wink.

4 stars because I would have like to see a better snack selection. I know... it's a winery, but there is nothing else near, no food or stores and while I often bring my own food, I still like to have something extra available. I'm a convenience seeker.

Prices are fair and this is a great date spot.< /Review>< user_name>
Sacita Duffy</user_name>
